class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw ia"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="io ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png?q=20" width="6719" height="3560"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="6719" height="3560"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/13438/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png" width="6719" height="3560" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*0EkxaCS4hXs-VZFMySTMMw.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h1 id="d4eb" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Introduction</h1><p id="2c51" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr kj"><span class="s kk kl km kn ko kp kq kr ks ct">A</span><em class="kt">mazon Elastic Kubernetes Service (Amazon EKS) is a managed service that makes it easy for you to run Kubernetes on AWS without needing to stand up or maintain your own Kubernetes control plane. Kubernetes is an open-source system for automating the deployment, scaling, and management of containerized applications.</em></p><p id="97f9" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Amazon EKS runs Kubernetes control plane instances across multiple Availability Zones to ensure high availability. Amazon EKS automatically detects and replaces unhealthy control plane instances, and it provides automated version upgrades and patching for them.</em></p><p id="b0ee" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Amazon EKS is also integrated with many AWS services to provide scalability and security for your applications, including the following:</em></p><ul class=""><li id="dd52" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">Amazon ECR for container images</em></strong></li><li id="d059" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">Elastic Load Balancing for load distribution</em></strong></li><li id="8de9" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">IAM for authentication</em></strong></li><li id="8cc0" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">Amazon VPC for isolation</em></strong></li></ul><p id="23fe" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Amazon EKS runs up-to-date versions of the open-source Kubernetes software, so you can use all the existing plugins and tooling from the Kubernetes community. Applications running on Amazon EKS are fully compatible with applications running on any standard Kubernetes environment, whether running in on-premises data centers or public clouds. This means that you can easily migrate any standard Kubernetes application to Amazon EKS without any code modification required.</em></p><h1 id="46fb" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Benefits</h1><ul class=""><li id="261b" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">High Availability</strong></li><li id="f76b" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Serverless Option</strong></li><li id="f78d" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">secure</strong></li><li id="dea0" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Built with community</strong></li></ul><h1 id="d768" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">How it works</h1><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw li"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="lj ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png?q=20" width="2892" height="1510"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="2892" height="1510"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/5784/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png" width="2892" height="1510" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*CKMOdVjiBdIWJUEvdjaIOg.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h2 id="1062" class="lk iu gj av ey ll lm jq ln lo ju lp lq jy lr ls kc lt lu kg lv cr">Companies adopting Amazon EKS</h2><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw lw"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="lx ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png?q=20" width="2858" height="1514"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="2858" height="1514"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/5716/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png" width="2858" height="1514" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*nACtPiUsYFxmE3Ktixuv9g.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h1 id="dd97" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Prerequisites</h1><ul class=""><li id="0963" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><em class="kt">Installing AWS CLI -The AWS Command Line Interface (CLI) is a unified tool to manage your AWS services. With just one tool to download and configure, you can control multiple AWS services from the command line and automate them through scripts.</em></li><li id="5ff7" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><em class="kt">Kubernetes uses a command-line utility called kubectl for communicating with the cluster API server. The kubectl binary is available in many operating system package managers, and this option is often much easier than a manual download and install process.</em></li><li id="fd68" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><code class="fj ly lz ma mb b"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">eksctl</em></strong></code><em class="kt"> is a simple CLI tool for creating clusters on EKS - Amazon&#x27;s new managed Kubernetes service for EC2. It is written in Go, uses CloudFormation, was created by </em><a href="https://www.weave.works/" class="bz do mc md me mf" rel="noopener nofollow"><em class="kt">Weaveworks</em></a><em class="kt"> and it welcomes contributions from the community. Install using this git </em><a href="https://github.com/weaveworks/eksctl" class="bz do mc md me mf" rel="noopener nofollow"><em class="kt">URL</em></a><em class="kt">.</em></li><li id="11c9" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><em class="kt">AWS CLI must be configured with you IAM or ROOT user and it also has the power to use the Roles service in AWS, for this, I suggest you create an IAM user with administrative access.</em></li></ul><h1 id="733a" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Weaveworks</h1><div class="mg mh mi mj mk ml"><a href="https://www.weave.works/" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow"><div class="mm n bp"><div class="mn n mo p mp mq"><h2 class="av ey mr ms ck mt cj hl mu hn cr">Weave Cloud</h2><div class="mv s"><h3 class="av aw ax ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">Weaveworks has been working with enterprises of all shapes and sizes to implement their Kubernetes platforms, across…</h3></div><div class="fq s"><h4 class="av aw mx ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">www.weave.works</h4></div></div><div class="my s"><div class="mz s na nb nc my nd ne ml"></div></div></div></a></div><div class="mg mh mi mj mk ml"><a href="https://github.com/weaveworks/eksctl" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow"><div class="mm n bp"><div class="mn n mo p mp mq"><h2 class="av ey mr ms ck mt cj hl mu hn cr">weaveworks/eksctl</h2><div class="mv s"><h3 class="av aw ax ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">eksctl is a simple CLI tool for creating clusters on EKS — Amazon’s new managed Kubernetes service for EC2. It is…</h3></div><div class="fq s"><h4 class="av aw mx ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">github.com</h4></div></div><div class="my s"><div class="nf s na nb nc my nd ne ml"></div></div></div></a></div><h1 id="6c2b" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Create an IAM</h1><p id="89bf" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Add permissions </em><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">AdministratorAccess</em></strong></p><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw ng"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="nh ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png?q=20" width="2872" height="1870"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="2872" height="1870"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/5744/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png" width="2872" height="1870" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*7IYnombxzhOK3h5PJ5OIOg.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><h1 id="dc2b" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Cluster Creation</h1><p id="e910" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Create a cluster just with one command and cluster can be created either by YAML file or by using CLI. Now, we will be doing using the YAML file and the requirements for creating a cluster you can put it in YAML file</em></p><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct  region: ap-south-1nodeGroups:<br/>   - name: ng1<br/>     desiredCapacity: 4<br/>     instanceType: t2.micro<br/>     ssh:<br/>        publicKeyName:  ekskey</strong></span></pre><p id="95c1" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">After creating this file we have to use a single command which will create entire Kubernetes setup.</em></p><pre class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="2c91" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">eksctl create cluster -f cluster.yml</strong></span></pre><figure class="ns nt fx fv fw nu nv av aw ax ay az">EC2 instance</figcaption></figure><pre class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="af66" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">eksctl get cluster</strong></span><span id="cc45" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nw nx ny nz oa no s np"><strong class="mb lc">aws eks update-kubeconfig --name &lt;cluster name&gt;</strong></span><span id="b6a0" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nw nx ny nz oa no s np"><strong class="mb lc">kubectl get nodes</strong></span></pre><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div id="0137" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Creating a PHP website using MYSQL Database</h1><p id="926c" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Kubectl supports the management of Kubernetes objects using a kustomization file. You can create a Secret by generators in kustomization.yaml.</em></p><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw od"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="oe ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png?q=20" width="1234" height="774"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="1234" height="774"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/2468/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png" width="1234" height="774" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*0N8Vm2EHpSAXz73_V3jSHQ.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><pre class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="402d" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">apiVersion: kustomize.config.k8s.io/v1beta1<br/>kind: Kustomization<br/>secretGenerator:<br/>  - name: mysql-pass<br/>    literals:<br/>        - password=redhat<br/>resources:<br/>  - mysql-deployment.yaml<br/>  - wordpress-deployment.yaml</strong></span></pre><h1 id="e161" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Manifest for SQL-deployment</h1><p id="4127" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">the manifest describes a single-instance MySQL Deployment. The MySQL container mounts the PersistentVolume at /var/lib/mysql. The MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD environment variable sets the database password from the Secret.</em></p><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw of"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="og ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/30/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png?q=20" width="904" height="1866"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="904" height="1866"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png" width="904" height="1866" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png 552w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1280/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png 640w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1400/1*z_3VtV4IpDcC3ZRuWYY4MA.png 700w" sizes="700px"/></noscript></div></div></div></div></figure><pre class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="38bf" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">apiVersion: v1<br/>kind: Service<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: wordpress-mysql<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  ports:<br/>    - port: 3306<br/>  selector:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>    tier: mysql<br/>  clusterIP: None<br/>---<br/>apiVersion: v1<br/>kind: PersistentVolumeClaim<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: mysql-pv-claim<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  accessModes:<br/>    - ReadWriteOnce<br/>  resources:<br/>    requests:<br/>      storage: 5Gi<br/>---<br/>apiVersion: apps/v1<br/>kind: Deployment<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: wordpress-mysql<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  selector:<br/>    matchLabels:<br/>      app: wordpress<br/>      tier: mysql<br/>  strategy:<br/>    type: Recreate<br/>  template:<br/>    metadata:<br/>      labels:<br/>        app: wordpress<br/>        tier: mysql<br/>    spec:<br/>      containers:<br/>      - image: mysql:5.6<br/>        name: mysql<br/>        env:<br/>        - name: MYSQL_ROOT_PASSWORD<br/>          valueFrom:<br/>            secretKeyRef:<br/>              name: mysql-pass<br/>              key: password<br/>        ports:<br/>        - containerPort: 3306<br/>          name: mysql<br/>        volumeMounts:<br/>        - name: mysql-persistent-storage<br/>          mountPath: /var/lib/mysql<br/>      volumes:<br/>      - name: mysql-persistent-storage<br/>        persistentVolumeClaim:<br/>          claimName: mysql-pv-claim</strong></span></pre><h1 id="74c5" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Manifest for WordPress Deployment</h1><p id="98a8" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">the manifest describes a single-instance WordPress Deployment. The WordPress container mounts the PersistentVolume at /var/www/html for website data files. The WORDPRESS_DB_HOST environment variable sets the name of the MySQL Service defined above, and WordPress will access the database by Service. The WORDPRESS_DB_PASSWORD environment variable sets the database password from the Secret kustomize generated.</em></p><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw of"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="og ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/30/1*7Q24VPsKYjZ0N0QglxYV7w.png?q=20" width="904" height="1866"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="904" height="1866"/><noscript><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/1808/1*7Q24VPsKYjZ0N0QglxYV7w.png" width="904" height="1866" srcSet="https://miro.medium.com/max/552/1*7Q24VPsKYjZ0N0QglxYV7w.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/1104/1*7Q24VPsKYjZ0N0QglxYV7w.png 552w, class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="c090" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc"><em class="kt">apiVersion: v1</em><br/>kind: Service<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: wordpress<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  ports:<br/>    - port: 80<br/>  selector:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>    tier: frontend<br/>  type: LoadBalancer<br/>---<br/>apiVersion: v1<br/>kind: PersistentVolumeClaim<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: wp-pv-claim<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  accessModes:<br/>    - ReadWriteOnce<br/>  resources:<br/>    requests:<br/>      storage: 5Gi<br/>---<br/>apiVersion: apps/v1<br/>kind: Deployment<br/>metadata:<br/>  name: wordpress<br/>  labels:<br/>    app: wordpress<br/>spec:<br/>  selector:<br/>    matchLabels:<br/>      app: wordpress<br/>      tier: frontend<br/>  strategy:<br/>    type: Recreate<br/>  template:<br/>    metadata:<br/>      labels:<br/>        app: wordpress<br/>        tier: frontend<br/>    spec:<br/>      containers:<br/>      - image: wordpress:4.8-apache<br/>        name: wordpress<br/>        env:<br/>        - name: WORDPRESS_DB_HOST<br/>          value: wordpress-mysql<br/>        - name: WORDPRESS_DB_PASSWORD<br/>          valueFrom:<br/>            secretKeyRef:<br/>              name: mysql-pass<br/>              key: password<br/>        ports:<br/>        - containerPort: 80<br/>          name: wordpress<br/>        volumeMounts:<br/>        - name: wordpress-persistent-storage<br/>          mountPath: /var/www/html<br/>      volumes:<br/>      - name: wordpress-persistent-storage<br/>        persistentVolumeClaim:<br/>          claimName: wp-pv-claim</strong></span></pre><p id="7da4" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv id="5b25" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">We just developed a fully managed PHP Website without any of our local environments, the nodes are in the AWS Cloud.</em></p><h1 id="41e4" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Helm</h1><p id="45f7" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Helm is a tool for managing Charts. Charts are packages of pre-configured Kubernetes resources.</em></p><div class="mg mh mi mj mk ml"><a href="https://hub.helm.sh/" target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow"><div class="mm n bp"><div class="mn n mo p mp mq"><h2 class="av ey mr ms ck mt cj hl mu hn cr">Helm Hub</h2><div class="mv s"><h3 class="av aw ax ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">Discover &amp; launch great Kubernetes-ready apps</h3></div><div class="fq s"><h4 class="av aw mx ay ck mw cj hl mu hn az">hub.helm.sh</h4></div></div></div></a></div><h1 id="28db" class="it iu gj av ey iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk cr">Uses of Helm</h1><ul class=""><li id="acbc" class="jl jm gj jn b jo jp jq jr js jt ju jv jw jx jy jz ka kb kc kd ke kf kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Find and use </strong><a href="https://hub.helm.sh/" class="bz do mc md me mf" rel="noopener nofollow"><strong class="jn lc">popular software packaged as Helm Charts</strong></a><strong class="jn lc"> to run in Kubernetes</strong></li><li id="83eb" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Share your own applications as Helm Charts</strong></li><li id="118c" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Create reproducible builds of your Kubernetes applications</strong></li><li id="4c81" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Intelligently manage your Kubernetes manifest files</strong></li><li id="fc4f" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ld jq jr js le ju jv jw lf jy jz ka lg kc kd ke lh kg kh ki kz la lb cr"><strong class="jn lc">Manage releases of Helm packages</strong></li></ul><p id="3ce6" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">Simply, you can assume this as we have created our website environment. And somebody also wants to use this environment so the second person also has to do this same setup again and again. To reduce this task helm provides Kubernetes help. We can install the popular environment within a second because of the power of container and Kubernetes.</em></p><p id="593a" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><em class="kt">So using the power of helm we are going to install two powerful environments one is Prometheus and the other one is Grafana. Prometheus is used to collect the metrics from the system and Grafana is a very popular Visualizing tool for Prometheus to see the system usage and many more things.</em></p><p id="5a1e" class="jl jm gj jn b jo ku jq jr js kv ju jv jw kw jy jz ka kx kc kd ke ky kg kh ki gb cr"><strong class="jn lc"><em class="kt">Download and install Helm and Tiller</em></strong></p><pre class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="8963" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">helm init</strong></span><span id="fdf3" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nw nx ny nz oa no s np"><strong class="mb lc">helm repo add stable </strong><a href="https://kubernetes-charts.storage.googleapis.com/" class="bz do mc md me mf" rel="noopener nofollow"><strong class="mb lc">https://kubernetes-charts.storage.googleapis.com/</strong></a></span><span id="1f64" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nw nx ny nz oa no s np"><strong class="mb lc">helm repo list</strong></span><span id="45c3" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nw nx ny nz oa no s np"><strong class="mb lc">helm repo update</strong></span></pre><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw on"><div class="in s ct fj"><div class="oo ip s"><div class="cp ik t u v dx aj ck il im"><img alt="Image for post" class="t u v dx aj iq ir is" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/60/1*e-wfb8ZvbzMMquEk9wwGMg.png?q=20" width="1948" height="590"/></div><img alt="Image for post" class="cp ik t u v dx aj c" width="1948" height="590"/><noscript><img class="ib ic id ie if nk nl nm"><span id="55c5" class="cr lk iu gj mb b ax nn no s np"><strong class="mb lc">kubectl -n kube-system create serviceaccount tiller</strong></span><span id="c13e" no s np"><strong class="mb lc">kubectl get pods --namespace kube-system</strong></span></pre><figure class="ib ic id ie if ig fv fw paragraph-image"><div class="ih ii ct ij aj"><div class="fv fw
